namespace = daoyu
daoyu.1 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_on
	desc = daoyu_on
	flavor = daoyu_on_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = ENABLE_IRONMAN
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_off
		set_global_variable = daoyu_on
		set_global_variable = daoyu_cheat
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.2 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CLOSE_LABEL
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_reconsideration
		default_option = yes
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_off
	}
}

#常用
daoyu.100 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_common
	flavor = daoyu_common_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = concept_journal_entry
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.140 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = africa_colonial_events.51.t
		trigger = { has_variable = ai_expedition_cooldown any_scope_character = { has_variable = expedition_leader_var } }
		change_variable = { name = expedition_progress add = 20 } remove_variable = ai_expedition_cooldown
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_money
		trigger = {
			or = {
				has_global_variable = daoyu_money_3
				has_global_variable = daoyu_money_4
				has_global_variable = daoyu_money_5
				has_global_variable = daoyu_money_6
				has_global_variable = daoyu_money_7
				has_global_variable = daoyu_money_8
				has_global_variable = daoyu_money_9
			}
			gold_reserves < gold_reserves_limit
		}
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_3 } add_treasury = 1000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_4 } add_treasury = 10000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_5 } add_treasury = 100000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_6 } add_treasury = 1000000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_7 } add_treasury = 10000000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_8 } add_treasury = 100000000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_9 } add_treasury = 1000000000 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = communism.3.a#忠诚必须绝对
		add_loyalists = { value = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_unemployed_disappear#清理失业
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			daoyu_auto_unemployed_effcet = yes
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_recognized_power_short#受认可
		trigger = { is_country_type = unrecognized }
		set_country_type = recognized
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = war_goal_independence#独立
		trigger = { aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = no }
		make_independent = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = obligation_events.4.t#更友善的形象
		trigger = { infamy >= 5 }
		change_infamy = -100
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = warlord_legitimacy#国家合法性
		trigger = { government_legitimacy <= 80 }
		add_modifier = { name = warlord_legitimacy months = -1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = warlord_legitimacy#国家合法性
		trigger = { government_legitimacy > 90 has_modifier = warlord_legitimacy }
		remove_modifier = warlord_legitimacy
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_literacy
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.110 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_colonial_integrity
		trigger = {
			any_state_region = {
				any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no owner = root }
				any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } }
				any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no owner = { not = { this = root is_country_type = decentralized } } }
			}
		}
		every_state_region = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no owner = root }
				any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } }
				any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no owner = { not = { this = root is_country_type = decentralized } } }
			}
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = { is_incorporated = no owner = { not = { this = root is_country_type = decentralized } } }
				set_state_owner = root
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporate_state#整合地区
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { is_treaty_port = no is_incorporated = no state_region = { not = { any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } } } } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { is_treaty_port = no is_incorporated = no state_region = { not = { any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } } } } set_state_type = incorporated }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_enactment_advance#立法推进
		trigger = { enacting_any_law = yes }
		add_enactment_modifier = { name = daoyu_auto_law_modifier }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = good_pollution_modifier#污染治理措施
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { state_region = { pollution_amount > 1 } } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { state_region = { pollution_amount > 1 } } state_region = { add_pollution = -100 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TRIGGER_IS_AT_WAR#战争中
		trigger = { is_at_war = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.120 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_settings#自给农提醒
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.130 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_promote_social_mobility_desc#鼓励民众争取更高的工作资质
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.150 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = interest_group_approval_add#利益集团支持度
		set_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.180 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_interest_group_political_strength#利益集团政治力量
		set_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.180 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_set_money_level
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.101 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}

		name = 3

#芥子气
daoyu.109 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:daoyu_tst_1
	title = mustard_gas
	desc = concept_generated_pollution
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_1 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_1 } } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_2 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_3 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_3 } } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_4 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_4 } } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_5 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_5 } } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_6 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_6 } } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_7 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_7 } } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_8 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_8 } } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_tst_9 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tst_9 } } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "middleeast_battlefield_trenches" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	duration = 3
	trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_modifier = mustard_gas not = { has_variable = daoyu_ignored_pollution_modifier } } }
	immediate = {
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_modifier = mustard_gas not = { has_variable = daoyu_ignored_pollution_modifier } } set_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_1 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_2 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_3 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_4 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_5 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_6 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_7 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_8 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_9 }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state } remove_variable = daoyu_mustard_gas_state }
	}
	duration = 3
	option = {
		name = ignored_pollution_modifier
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_modifier = mustard_gas not = { has_variable = daoyu_ignored_pollution_modifier } } set_variable = { name = daoyu_ignored_pollution_modifier months = 12 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = good_pollution_modifier
		default_option = yes
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_modifier = mustard_gas not = { has_variable = daoyu_ignored_pollution_modifier } } remove_modifier = mustard_gas remove_modifier = mustard_gas }
	}
}

daoyu.110 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_literacy
	flavor = daoyu_common_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = RADICALISM_HIGH
		effect_starting_pop_literacy_high = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RADICALISM_VERY_HIGH
		effect_starting_pop_literacy_very_high = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RADICALISM_EXTREME
		every_scope_pop = { set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = { value = 0.8 if = { limit = { state = { is_incorporated = no } } multiply = 0.5 } } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RADICALISM_CRITICAL
		every_scope_pop = { set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = { value = 1 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#战争中
daoyu.120 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = TRIGGER_IS_AT_WAR_NOCONTEXT
	flavor = daoyu_common_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_american_civil_war.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/american_civil_war"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = concept_war_support#战争支持度
		trigger = { any_scope_war = { has_war_support = { target = ROOT value < 80 } } }
		random_scope_war = { limit = { has_war_support = { target = ROOT value < 80 } } add_war_war_support = { target = ROOT value = 10 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.120 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_war_exhaustion#厌战度
		trigger = { any_scope_war = { has_war_exhaustion = { target = ROOT value > 0 } } }
		random_scope_war = { limit = { has_war_exhaustion = { target = ROOT value > 0 } } add_war_exhaustion = { target = ROOT value = -10 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.120 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#自给农提醒
daoyu.130 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_settings
	flavor = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_settings_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = TICKTASK_RATE_WEEK#每周一次
		set_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week remove_variable = daoyu_auto_create_peasants
		if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week_on } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.132 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TICKTASK_RATE_MONTH#每月一次
		set_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_month remove_variable = daoyu_auto_create_peasants
		if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_month_on } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.133 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_add_week#每周一次
		set_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week set_variable = daoyu_auto_create_peasants
		if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week_on } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.132 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_add_month#每月一次
		set_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_month set_variable = daoyu_auto_create_peasants
		if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_month_on } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.133 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = DISMISS#关闭
		remove_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week
		remove_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_month
		remove_variable = daoyu_auto_create_peasants
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}

#自给农提醒
daoyu.131 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:daoyu_peasants_exhaustion
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion
	flavor = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_located
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 3
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = { not = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } } has_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state }
			remove_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state
			save_scope_as = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bureaucracy.3.c
		default_option = yes
	}
}
daoyu.132 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week }
			set_variable = { name = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week_on weeks = 1 }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.132 weeks = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = daoyu_auto_create_peasants }
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { not = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } } }
					if = { limit = { free_arable_land < 5 } state_region = { add_arable_land = 5 } }
					create_pop = { size = 2000 working_adult_ratio = 1 pop_type = peasants }
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } not = { has_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state } }
					set_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state
				}
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { not = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } } has_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state }
					root = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.131 popup = yes } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

daoyu.180 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { } desc = modifier_interest_group_approval_add }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } desc = daoyu_interest_group_political_strength }
		}
	}
	flavor = daoyu_cheat
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all_ig_modifiers#删除所有利益集团修正
		trigger = {
			or = {
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval any_country = { any_interest_group = { or = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval_SUB has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval_ADD } } } }
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str any_country = { any_interest_group = { or = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str_SUB has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str_ADD } } } }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval } every_country = { every_interest_group = { daoyu_remove_interest_group_approval_effcet = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } every_country = { every_interest_group = { daoyu_remove_interest_group_pol_str_effcet = yes } } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_ig_modifiers
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_armed_forces#军队
		trigger = { any_interest_group = { is_interest_group_type = ig_armed_forces } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_ig_armed_forces
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_landowners#地主
		trigger = { any_interest_group = { is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_ig_landowners
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_devout#虔信者
		trigger = { any_interest_group = { is_interest_group_type = ig_devout } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_ig_devout
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_industrialists#实业家
		trigger = { any_interest_group = { is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_ig_industrialists
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_intelligentsia#知识分子
		trigger = { any_interest_group = { is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_ig_intelligentsia
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_petty_bourgeoisie#小市民
		trigger = { any_interest_group = { is_interest_group_type = ig_petty_bourgeoisie } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_trade_unions#工会
		trigger = { any_interest_group = { is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_ig_trade_unions
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_rural_folk#乡村民众
		trigger = { any_interest_group = { is_interest_group_type = ig_rural_folk } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_ig_rural_folk
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_ig_modifiers } remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_all_ig_modifiers trigger_event = { id = daoyu.180 popup = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.181 popup = yes } }
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.200 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_characters
	flavor = daoyu_cheat
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_manage_character#管理角色
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.210 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_character#创建角色
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_210 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ideology_royalist#保皇主义者
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_210 } has_law = law_type:law_monarchy any_scope_character = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_royalist } } }
		every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_royalist } } set_ideology = ideology:ideology_royalist }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ideology_republican_leader#共和主义者
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_210 }
			root = { or = { has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic } }
			any_scope_character = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_leader } }
		}
		every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_leader } } set_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_leader }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ideology_theocrat#神权政治主义者
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_210 } has_law = law_type:law_theocracy any_scope_character = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_theocrat } } }
		every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_theocrat } } set_ideology = ideology:ideology_theocrat }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ideology_communist#共产主义者
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_210 } has_law = law_type:law_council_republic any_scope_character = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist } } }
		every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist } } set_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_unified_ideology#统一意识形态同君主
		#trigger = { ruler = { nor = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_royalist has_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_leader has_ideology = ideology:ideology_theocrat has_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist } } }
		daoyu_change_ideology_same_ruler_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = traitors_executed_propaganda#处决背叛嫌疑人
		trigger = { any_character = { has_variable = daoyu_betrayal_will_die owner = { is_ai = yes } } }
		every_character = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_betrayal_will_die } kill_character = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CHARACTER_HISTORICAL_HEADER#历史角色
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.290 popup = yes } }

	type = country_event

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_filter_army } remove_global_variable = daoyu_filter_army }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_filter_fleet } remove_global_variable = daoyu_filter_fleet }
		if = {
			limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } }
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_1 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_2 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_3
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_4 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_5 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_6
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_7 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_8 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcr_9
		}
		random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_life_experience#人生经验
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_experience = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = religious_orthodocy_enforced_mod#强迫信仰
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.230 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_character_traits#角色特质
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.240 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_ideology#意识形态
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.250 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = je_ethno_nationalist#我们的民族我们的文化
		trigger = { not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_target_character.culture } }
		daoyu_change_target_character_culture = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = assassination_events.5.t#刺杀
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.260 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = modifier_interest_group_approval_add#利益集团支持度
		set_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.221 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_interest_group_political_strength#利益集团政治力量
		set_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.221 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all_ig_modifiers#删除利益集团所有修正
		trigger = {
			or = {
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval any_country = { any_interest_group = { or = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval_SUB has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval_ADD } } } }
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str any_country = { any_interest_group = { or = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str_SUB has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str_ADD } } } }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval } every_country = { every_interest_group = { daoyu_remove_interest_group_approval_effcet = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } every_country = { every_interest_group = { daoyu_remove_interest_group_pol_str_effcet = yes } } }

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation.1 popup = yes } }

		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = admiral } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_filter_fleet set_variable = daoyu_page_01
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation.1 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { remove_trait = daoyu_target_character }

	}

daoyu.240 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_character_traits
	flavor = daoyu_target_character_get_name
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_general remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_admiral remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_politician
		random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_trait
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.241 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_personality_traits
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.242 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_skill_traits
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.243 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_conditions_traits
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.244 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_general_modifier
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = general } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.245 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_admiral_modifier
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = admiral } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.246 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_personality_traits
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_character_get_name }

daoyu.243 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_skill_traits
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_character_get_name }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_check_more }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = daoyu_243
		random_character = {
			limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character }
			save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character
			if = { limit = { has_trait = traditionalist_commander } remove_trait = traditionalist_commander add_trait = celebrity_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = popular_commander } remove_trait = popular_commander add_trait = celebrity_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = stalwart_defender } remove_trait = stalwart_defender add_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = trench_rat } remove_trait = trench_rat add_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_artillery_commander } remove_trait = basic_artillery_commander add_trait = expert_artillery_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_artillery_commander } remove_trait = experienced_artillery_commander add_trait = expert_artillery_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_offensive_planner } remove_trait = basic_offensive_planner add_trait = expert_offensive_planner }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_offensive_planner } remove_trait = experienced_offensive_planner add_trait = expert_offensive_planner }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_defensive_strategist } remove_trait = basic_defensive_strategist add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_defensive_strategist } remove_trait = experienced_defensive_strategist add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_naval_commander } remove_trait = basic_naval_commander add_trait = expert_naval_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_naval_commander } remove_trait = experienced_naval_commander add_trait = expert_naval_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = convoy_raider_commander } remove_trait = convoy_raider_commander add_trait = expert_convoy_raider }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_convoy_raider } remove_trait = experienced_convoy_raider add_trait = expert_convoy_raider }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_diplomat } remove_trait = basic_diplomat add_trait = masterful_diplomat }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_diplomat } remove_trait = experienced_diplomat add_trait = masterful_diplomat }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_colonial_administrator } remove_trait = basic_colonial_administrator add_trait = expert_colonial_administrator }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_colonial_administrator } remove_trait = experienced_colonial_administrator add_trait = expert_colonial_administrator }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_political_operator } remove_trait = basic_political_operator add_trait = expert_political_operator }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_political_operator } remove_trait = experienced_political_operator add_trait = expert_political_operator }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = inspirational_orator } remove_trait = inspirational_orator add_trait = firebrand }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = demagogue } remove_trait = demagogue add_trait = firebrand }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ACHIEVEMENT_FILTER_BUTTON_ALL
		scope:daoyu_target_character = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = yes is_heir = yes }
				add_trait = traditionalist_commander add_trait = expert_political_operator add_trait = expert_colonial_administrator add_trait = firebrand 
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_role = general }
				add_trait = pillager add_trait = surveyor add_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist add_trait = resupply_commander add_trait = forest_commander add_trait = plains_commander
				add_trait = mountain_commander add_trait = expert_artillery_commander add_trait = expert_offensive_planner add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
				add_trait = traditionalist_commander
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_role = admiral }
				add_trait = expert_naval_commander add_trait = expert_convoy_raideradd_trait = dockyard_master add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
				add_trait = traditionalist_commander
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_role = politician }
				add_trait = expert_political_operator add_trait = firebrand add_trait = literary
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_role = agitator }
				add_trait = expert_political_operator add_trait = firebrand add_trait = erudite add_trait = engineer add_trait = literary
			}
			add_trait = explorer add_trait = erudite add_trait = engineer add_trait = master_bureaucrat add_trait = celebrity_commander add_trait = masterful_diplomat 
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = explorer
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = explorer } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = explorer }
	}
	option = {
		name = erudite
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = erudite } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = erudite }
	}
	option = {
		name = engineer
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = engineer } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = engineer }
	}
	option = {
		name = master_bureaucrat
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = master_bureaucrat } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = master_bureaucrat }
	}
	option = {
		name = celebrity_commander
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = celebrity_commander } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = celebrity_commander }
	}
	option = {
		name = literary
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { is_commander = no not = { has_trait = literary } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = literary }
	}
	option = {
		name = masterful_diplomat
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = masterful_diplomat } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = masterful_diplomat }
	}
	option = {
		name = traditionalist_commander
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { nor = { has_role = agitator has_role = politician }  not = { has_trait = traditionalist_commander } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = traditionalist_commander }
	}
	option = {

daoyu.251 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = concept_ideologies
	desc = tutorial_lesson_button_show_more
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_character_get_name }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_check_only_one }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character }
			save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character
		}
		if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { nor = { has_role = agitator has_ideology = ideology:﻿ideology_moderate } } } set_global_variable = can_set_ideology_moderate }
	}
	option = { name = ONLY_SHOW_AVAILABLE set_global_variable = daoyu_250 }
	option = { name = ideology_moderate trigger = { daoyu_ideology_moderate = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } }
	option = { name = ideology_traditionalist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_traditionalist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_traditionalist } }
	option = { name = ideology_atheist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_atheist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_atheist } }
	option = { name = ideology_republican_leader trigger = { daoyu_ideology_republican_leader = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_leader } }
	option = { name = ideology_radical trigger = { daoyu_ideology_radical = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_radical } }
	option = { name = ideology_reformer trigger = { daoyu_ideology_reformer = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_reformer } }
	option = { name = ideology_feminist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_feminist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_feminist } }
	option = { name = ideology_abolitionist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_abolitionist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_abolitionist } }
	option = { name = ideology_slaver trigger = { daoyu_ideology_slaver = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_slaver } }
	option = { name = ideology_pacifist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_pacifist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_pacifist } }
	option = { name = ideology_jingoist_leader trigger = { daoyu_ideology_jingoist_leader = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_jingoist_leader } }
	option = { name = ideology_royalist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_royalist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_royalist } }
	option = { name = ideology_social_democrat trigger = { daoyu_ideology_social_democrat = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_social_democrat } }
	option = { name = ideology_communist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_communist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist } }
	option = { name = ideology_vanguardist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_vanguardist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_vanguardist } }
	option = { name = ideology_fascist trigger = { daoyu_ideology_fascist = no } scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_fascist } }
	option = {
		name = ENCYCLOPEDIAGE_NEXT_PAGE
		set_global_variable = daoyu_252
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
	}
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = can_set_ideology_moderate
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_250 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_250 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.250 popup = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_252 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_252 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.252 popup = yes } }
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	placement = root

	desc = assassination_events.5.t
	flavor = daoyu_target_character_get_name
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = assassination_ruler_scope }
	}
	option = {
		name = assassination_events.8.a
		hidden_effect = { scope:assassination_ruler_scope = { remove_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		scope:assassination_ruler_scope = { kill_character = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = assassination_events.6.a
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.271 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_create_character
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { or = { has_variable = daoyu_create_general has_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } desc = daoyu_mf_1 } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_create_general } desc = ai_goal_recruit_generals } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } desc = ai_goal_recruit_admirals } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_create_politician } desc = concept_politician } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_create_agitator } desc = concept_agitator } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_create_ruler } desc = concept_ruler } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		remove_variable = daoyu_ig_armed_forces remove_variable = daoyu_ig_devout remove_variable = daoyu_ig_industrialists remove_variable = daoyu_ig_intelligentsia
		remove_variable = daoyu_ig_landowners remove_variable = daoyu_ig_petty_bourgeoisie remove_variable = daoyu_ig_rural_folk remove_variable = daoyu_ig_trade_unions
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_armed_forces
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_armed_forces" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_devout
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_devout" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_industrialists
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_industrialists" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_intelligentsia
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_intelligentsia" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_landowners
		set_variable = daoyu_noble daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_landowners" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_petty_bourgeoisie" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_rural_folk
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_rural_folk" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_trade_unions
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_trade_unions" }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } }
		remove_variable = daoyu_create_general remove_variable = daoyu_create_admiral remove_variable = daoyu_create_politician remove_variable = concept_agitator
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions }
		remove_variable = daoyu_create_general remove_variable = daoyu_create_admiral
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions nor = { has_variable = daoyu_create_general has_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } }
			clear_saved_scope = daoyu_mf_1 remove_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions or = { has_variable = daoyu_create_general has_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } }
			if = {
				random_scope_character = {
					limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character }
					transfer_to_formation = scope:daoyu_mf_1
				}
			}
			clear_saved_scope = daoyu_mf_1
			remove_variable = daoyu_create_general
			remove_variable = daoyu_create_admiral
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { or = { has_variable = daoyu_create_general has_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } }
			remove_variable = daoyu_create_general remove_variable = daoyu_create_admiral trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { or = { has_variable = daoyu_create_politician has_variable = daoyu_create_agitator has_variable = daoyu_create_ruler } }
			remove_variable = daoyu_create_politician remove_variable = daoyu_create_agitator remove_variable = daoyu_create_ruler trigger_event = { id = daoyu.240 popup = yes }
		}
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.280 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = ai_goal_set_generals_orders
	flavor = daoyu_cheat
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_skill_traits
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_general_modifier }
			any_scope_general = {
				is_ruler = no
				nor = {
					has_trait = pillager has_trait = surveyor has_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist has_trait = resupply_commander has_trait = forest_commander has_trait = plains_commander
					has_trait = mountain_commander has_trait = expert_artillery_commander has_trait = expert_offensive_planner has_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
				}
			}
		}
		every_scope_general = {
			limit = { is_ruler = no }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_trait = trench_rat remove_trait = basic_artillery_commander remove_trait = experienced_artillery_commander remove_trait = experienced_defensive_strategist
				remove_trait = basic_offensive_planner remove_trait = experienced_offensive_planner remove_trait = basic_defensive_strategist remove_trait = stalwart_defender
			}
			add_trait = pillager add_trait = surveyor add_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist add_trait = resupply_commander add_trait = forest_commander add_trait = plains_commander
			add_trait = mountain_commander add_trait = expert_artillery_commander add_trait = expert_offensive_planner add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist set_variable = daoyu_betrayal_will_die
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.280 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_personality_traits
		set_global_variable = daoyu_general_personality_traits
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.282 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_goal_promote_generals#晋升陆军将领
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_general_modifier } any_scope_general = { commander_rank < 5 is_ruler = no } }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 2 } } every_scope_general = { limit = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 2 } add_commander_rank = 1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 3 } } every_scope_general = { limit = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 3 } add_commander_rank = 1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 4 } } every_scope_general = { limit = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 4 } add_commander_rank = 1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 5 } } every_scope_general = { limit = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 5 } add_commander_rank = 1 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.280 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_general_modifier
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_general_modifier } any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_general_modifier
		every_scope_general = {
			limit = { is_ruler = no }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
				remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.280 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RADICALISM_LOW

		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_general_personality_traits } every_scope_general = { add_trait = pious } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_admiral_personality_traits } every_scope_admiral = { add_trait = pious } }
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_general_personality_traits } remove_global_variable = daoyu_general_personality_traits trigger_event = { id = daoyu.280 popup = yes } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_admiral_personality_traits } remove_global_variable = daoyu_admiral_personality_traits trigger_event = { id = daoyu.281 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.300 = {

		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_country_desc }

	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0

	}

		name = NO_OBJECTIVE#你未选择目标
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }

		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标

		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}

		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_other_country#失业人口送目标国家

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_root_join_target_country_power_bloc#加入国家集团

		join_power_bloc = scope:daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}

		name = daoyu_target_country_join_root_power_bloc#加入国家集团

		scope:daoyu_target_country = { join_power_bloc = root }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_power_bloc_leverage#影响
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes }
		power_bloc = { add_leverage = { target = scope:daoyu_target_country value = 100 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.360 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_diplomatic_play#外交博弈
		if = { limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.320 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.301 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {

	}

daoyu.302 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_other_country
	flavor = daoyu_target_country_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality }
			random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } save_scope_as = daoyu_high_growth_mortality }
			random_state = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } save_scope_as = daoyu_high_growth_mortality_state }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } } }
			random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID#目标国家无效
		trigger = { nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_daoyu_target_country#失业人口送目标国家
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } } any_scope_state = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } move_pop = scope:daoyu_target_country.capital } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_daoyu_high_growth_mortality#失业人口送目标国家
		trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } any_scope_state = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } move_pop = scope:daoyu_high_growth_mortality_state } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_add_pop_growth_mortality#死亡率
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country any_scope_state = { count > 1 } } }
			hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.303 popup = yes } }
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
				set_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality
				every_scope_state = { add_modifier = { name = daoyu_high_growth_mortality years = -1 } }
			}
			set_global_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality
			hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_daoyu_high_growth_mortality_remove_pop_growth_mortality#死亡率
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality }
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality }
			remove_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality
		}
		every_state = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } remove_modifier = daoyu_high_growth_mortality }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.320 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_diplomatic_play
	flavor = daoyu_target_country_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = NO_OBJECTIVE#你未选择目标
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.320 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_create_diplomatic_play_against_root#处理外交博弈
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { create_diplomatic_play = { target_country = root war = no type = dp_open_market } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_diplomatic_play_make_puppet_against_target_country_war_now#傀儡
		trigger = {
			aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
			not = { is_subject_of = scope:daoyu_target_country country_rank = rank_value:great_power }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
				not = { is_subject_of = root }
			}	
		}
		create_diplomatic_play = { target_country = scope:daoyu_target_country war = yes type = dp_make_puppet }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_diplomatic_play_annex_subject_against_target_country_war_now#吞并附属国
		trigger = {
			not = { is_country_type = decentralized }
			aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				is_direct_subject_of = root
				or = {
					has_diplomatic_pact = { who = root type = dominion }
					has_diplomatic_pact = { who = root type = puppet }
					has_diplomatic_pact = { who = root type = vassal }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_diplomatic_play_annex_war_against_target_country_war_now#吞并国家
		trigger = {
			aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
			not = { is_country_type = decentralized is_subject_of = scope:daoyu_target_country }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { is_country_type = decentralized is_subject_of = root }
				aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
			}	
		}
		create_diplomatic_play = { target_country = scope:daoyu_target_country war = yes type = dp_annex_war }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
}

			not = { is_subject_of = scope:daoyu_target_country }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				has_modifier = daoyu_target_country is_at_war = no
				aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
				not = { is_subject_of = root has_war_with = root }
				any_scope_state = { any_neighbouring_state = { owner = { has_war_with = root } } }
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { violate_sovereignty_join = { violator = root target = scope:daoyu_target_country join_violator = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = increase_relations#改善关系

daoyu.331 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_annex_target_country
	flavor = daoyu_target_country_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { remove_global_variable = daoyu_331 random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country } annex = scope:daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.330 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.340 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_transfer_state
	flavor = daoyu_target_country_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_cede_state_to_other_county#赠予他国地区
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.341 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_cede_other_county_state#他国割让地区
		trigger = { any_country = { any_scope_state = { count > 1 } has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
			if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { is_sea_adjacent = yes count = 1 } } every_scope_state = { limit = { is_sea_adjacent = no } set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
			else = { every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.345 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_claim_other_county_state#宣称他国地区
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country any_scope_state = { not = { has_claim_by = root } } } }
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
			every_scope_state = { limit = { not = { has_claim_by = root } } set_variable = daoyu_potential_target }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.347 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#赠予他国地区
daoyu.341 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_cede_state_to_other_county
	flavor = daoyu_states_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = NO_OBJECTIVE
		trigger = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } }
			or = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.341 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } }
			any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		}
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_cede_state set_state_owner = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.341 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporated_states
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } remove_variable = daoyu_cede_state set_state_type = incorporated } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_unincorporated_states
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } remove_variable = daoyu_cede_state } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } } }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_agricultural_expansion#投资农业
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_agricultural_expansion } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_agricultural_expansion }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_resource_expansion#扩大资源产业
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_resource_expansion } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_resource_expansion }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_industrial_expansion#工业化
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_industrial_expansion } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_industrial_expansion }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_colonial_extraction#殖民地开采
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_colonial_extraction } is_subject = yes is_country_type = colonial } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_colonial_extraction }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_plantation_economy#种植园经济
		trigger = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_plantation_economy }
				or = {
					capital.region = sr:region_dixie
					country_is_in_south_america = yes
					country_is_in_central_america = yes
					country_is_in_india = yes
					country_is_in_southeast_asia = yes
					country_is_in_africa = yes	
					country_is_in_east_asia = yes	
					country_is_in_middle_east = yes	
				}
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_plantation_economy }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_placate_population#安抚群众
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_placate_population } has_law = law_type:law_traditionalism } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_placate_population }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
	}
	after = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.350 popup = yes } }
}

#分裂
daoyu.380 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_all_country_division
	flavor = daoyu_all_country_division_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#确认
		trigger = { game_date = 1836.1.1 not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_all_country_division } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_all_country_division
		every_country = { limit = { or = { and = { is_subject = yes top_overlord = { is_ai = no } } is_ai = no } } set_variable = daoyu_player }
		every_country = { limit = { is_subject = yes not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } make_independent = yes }
		every_state = {
			limit = { owner = { any_scope_state { count = 1 } } state_region = { any_scope_state { is_capital = no owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } any_scope_state { count > 1 } } } } }
			state_region = {
				prev.owner = {
					every_state = { limit = { state_region = prev.capital.state_region is_capital = no owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } any_scope_state { count > 1 } } } set_state_owner = prev }
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } any_scope_state = { count > 2 } } daoyu_create_country_effect = yes }
		every_country = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } any_scope_state = { count > 2 } } daoyu_create_country_effect = yes }
		every_state = {
			limit = { owner = { any_scope_state { count = 1 } } state_region = { any_scope_state { is_capital = no owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } any_scope_state { count > 1 } } } } }
			state_region = {
				prev.owner = {
					set_variable = daoyu_victorian_century
					every_state = {
						limit = { state_region = prev.capital.state_region is_capital = no owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } any_scope_state { count > 1 } } }
						set_state_owner = prev
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { exists = c:OCC } every_state = { limit = { is_homeland_of_country_cultures = c:OCC owner = { any_scope_state = { count > 3 } not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:OCC } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:ENG } s:STATE_EAST_ANGLIA = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:ENG } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:ENG } s:STATE_WEST_COUNTRY = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:ENG } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:ALD } s:STATE_ALGIERS = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:ALD } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:MOR } s:STATE_AL_RIF = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:MOR } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:KON } s:STATE_NORTH_ANGOLA = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:KON } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:MAD } s:STATE_INDIAN_OCEAN_TERRITORY = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:MAD } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:SMI } s:STATE_OSTROBOTHNIA = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:SMI } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:FIN } s:STATE_EAST_KARELIA = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:FIN } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:HOH } s:STATE_ALSACE_LORRAINE = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:HOH } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:WUR } s:STATE_WURTTEMBERG = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:WUR } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:OLD } s:STATE_EAST_PRUSSIA = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:OLD } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:HAN } s:STATE_HANNOVER = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:HAN } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:HAM } s:STATE_POSEN = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:HAM } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:BRE } s:STATE_ELBE = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:BRE } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:MST } s:STATE_SILESIA = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:MST } } }

		if = { limit = { exists = c:BTN } s:STATE_MOLUCCAS = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:BTN } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = c:SLW } s:STATE_CELEBES = { every_scope_state = { limit = { owner = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_player } } } set_state_owner = c:SLW } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.381 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	}
	option = {

		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.390 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#移除目标国家
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.390 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_create_radicals
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } every_scope_state = { daoyu_add_radicals_in_state_effect = yes } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.390 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_all_country_spring
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_country_add_radicals } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.391 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.400 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_power_bloc
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { is_in_power_bloc = no } desc = daoyu_no_power_bloc } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes } } desc = daoyu_target_country_power_bloc } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes } desc = daoyu_root_power_bloc } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_root_join_target_country_power_bloc#加入国家集团
		trigger = { is_in_power_bloc = no exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes } }
		join_power_bloc = scope:daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_join_root_power_bloc#加入国家集团
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_in_power_bloc = no } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { join_power_bloc = root }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_power_bloc_modifier#国家集团修正
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.410 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_power_bloc_leverage#影响
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes } } }
		power_bloc = { add_leverage = { target = scope:daoyu_target_country value = 100 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_power_bloc_cohesion#凝聚力
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes power_bloc = { current_cohesion_percentage < 1 } }
		power_bloc = { add_cohesion_percent = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ADD_NEW_PRINCIPLE#添加原则
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.420 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_principle#移除原则
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_principle
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.420 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions
		default_option = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
		default_option = yes
	}
}

		daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = { PRI = "colonial_offices" }
	}
	option = {
		name = principle_group_foreign_investment#外国投资
		trigger = { daoyu_has_principle = { PRI = "foreign_investment" } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = { PRI = "foreign_investment" }
	}
	option = {
		name = principle_group_creative_legislature#创意立法
		trigger = { daoyu_has_principle = { PRI = "creative_legislature" } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = { PRI = "creative_legislature" }
	}
	option = {
		name = principle_group_freedom_of_movement#迁徙自由
		trigger = { daoyu_has_principle = { PRI = "freedom_of_movement" } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = { PRI = "freedom_of_movement" }
	}
	option = {
		name = principle_group_divine_economics#神圣经济学
		trigger = { daoyu_has_principle = { PRI = "divine_economics" } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = { PRI = "divine_economics" }
	}
	option = {
		name = principle_group_exploit_members#剥削成员国
		trigger = { daoyu_has_principle = { PRI = "exploit_members" } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = { PRI = "exploit_members" }
	}
	option = {
		name = principle_group_sacred_civics#神圣公民
		trigger = { daoyu_has_principle = { PRI = "sacred_civics" } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = { PRI = "sacred_civics" }
	}
	option = {
		name = principle_group_ideological_truth#意识形态真理
		trigger = { daoyu_has_principle = { PRI = "ideological_truth" } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_principle = { PRI = "ideological_truth" }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_principle
		set_variable = daoyu_return
		default_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_return } remove_variable = daoyu_return trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.420 popup = yes } }
	}
}
