daoyu.510 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu } desc = law_cultural_exclusion }#文化排斥
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu } desc = law_multicultural }#文化多元
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } desc = russification_modifier }#民族同化
		}
	}
	flavor = daoyu_cheat
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.510 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID#目标国家无效
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.510 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#移除目标国家
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.510 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_get_name
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } } trigger_event = { id = dculo.70 popup = yes } }
			else = {
				daoyu_primary_culture_count_effect = yes
				if = { limit = { var:daoyu_primary_culture_count = 1 } trigger_event = { id = dculo.70 popup = yes } }
				else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_root_get_name
		set_variable = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } } trigger_event = { id = dculo.70 popup = yes } }
			else = {
				daoyu_primary_culture_count_effect = yes
				if = { limit = { var:daoyu_primary_culture_count = 1 } trigger_event = { id = dculo.70 popup = yes } }
				else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.520 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = religious_orthodocy_enforced_mod
	flavor = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population } } desc = daoyu_root_get_name }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name }
		}
		first_valid = { desc = religious_orthodocy_enforced_mod }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } }
			set_global_variable = daoyu_520
		}
		if = {
			limit= { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
			random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country#目标国家
		trigger = { nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion has_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population } }
		if = { limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } set_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population }
	}
	option = {
		name = catholic#天主教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "catholic" }
	}
	option = {
		name = protestant#新教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "protestant" }
	}
	option = {
		name = orthodox#东正教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "orthodox" }
	}
	option = {
		name = oriental_orthodox#东方正统教会
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "oriental_orthodox" }
	}
	option = {
		name = sunni#逊尼派
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "sunni" }
	}
	option = {
		name = shiite#什叶派
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "shiite" }
	}
	option = {
		name = jewish#犹太教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "jewish" }
	}
	option = {
		name = mahayana#大乘佛教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "mahayana" }
	}
	option = {
		name = gelugpa#格鲁派
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "gelugpa" }
	}
	option = {
		name = theravada#上座部佛教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "theravada" }
	}
	option = {
		name = confucian#儒家
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "confucian" }
	}
	option = {
		name = hindu#印度教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "hindu" }
	}
	option = {
		name = shinto#神道教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "shinto" }
	}
	option = {
		name = sikh#锡克教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "sikh" }
	}
	option = {
		name = animist#泛灵论
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "animist" }
	}
	option = {
		name = atheist#无神论
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "atheist" }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion not = { has_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } }
			set_global_variable = dculo_10
		}
		else = { remove_global_variable = daoyu_520 }
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_520 } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.520 popup = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dculo_10 } trigger_event = { id = dculo.10 popup = yes } }
		else = {
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes }
			#一球一族一教
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion not = { has_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } }
				every_scope_character = { change_character_culture = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture }
				daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = yes
				add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture
				every_scope_state = {
					every_scope_pop = { if = { limit = { pop_has_primary_culture = no } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture } } }
				}
				every_state = {
					daoyu_remove_homeland_effect = yes
					state_region = { add_homeland = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture }
				}
				set_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion
				random_country = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.509 } }
			}
		}
	}
}
#标记文化
daoyu.570 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_mark_target_culture
	flavor = daoyu_mark_target_culture_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture }
			set_global_variable = daoyu_save_mark_target_culture_effect
			daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_save_mark_target_culture_effect
		}
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_mark_target_culture#删除标记文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture
		set_global_variable = dculo_remove_global_variable_effect
		daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
		remove_global_variable = dculo_remove_global_variable_effect
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_mark_target_culture#标记文化
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dculo.10 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_add_primary_culture_mark_target_culture_for_root#本国加入主流文化标记文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } }
		add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_primary_culture_change_into_mark_target_culture_for_root#标记文化同化本国主流文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { pop_has_primary_culture = yes } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
		daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = yes
		add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_owned_state_add_cultural_community#添加文化社群
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture any_scope_state = { not = { has_cultural_community = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { not = { has_cultural_community = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } }
			add_cultural_community = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_daoyu_target_state#目标地区
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.572 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_add_primary_culture_mark_target_culture_for_target_country#目标国家加入主流文化标记文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_primary_culture_change_into_mark_target_culture_for_target_country#标记文化同化目标国家主流文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { pop_has_primary_culture = yes } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
			daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = yes
			add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_state#目标国家的地区
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.571 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
	}

		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_obsession } desc = concept_obsession } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_banned } desc = daoyu_banned } }

		name = REMOVE_FROM_GOVERNMENT_SHORT#移除
		trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_obsession } set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_cultural_obsession }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_banned } set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_banned_goods }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.582 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.580 popup = yes } }
	}

			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_cultural_obsession } desc = REMOVE_FROM_GOVERNMENT_SHORT }

		}
		first_valid = {

			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_banned } desc = daoyu_banned }
		}
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { is_ai = no } desc = MARKET_GOODS } }
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_military } } desc = MILITARY_GOODS }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_staple } } desc = CONSUMER_GOODS }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_industrial } } desc = INDUSTRIAL_GOODS }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_luxury } } desc = LUXURY_GOODS }
		}
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_art_gallery.bk2" }

		name = MILITARY_GOODS#军用
		trigger = {
			not = { has_variable = daoyu_military has_variable = daoyu_staple has_variable = daoyu_industrial has_variable = daoyu_luxury }

				daoyu_cultural_obsession_trigger = { GOODS = "ammunition" }
				daoyu_cultural_obsession_trigger = { GOODS = "small_arms" }
				daoyu_cultural_obsession_trigger = { GOODS = "artillery" }
				daoyu_cultural_obsession_trigger = { GOODS = "tanks" }
				daoyu_cultural_obsession_trigger = { GOODS = "aeroplanes" }

				daoyu_cultural_obsession_trigger = { GOODS = "ironclads" }
			}
		}
		set_variable = daoyu_military

#一键洗地
daoyu.590 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect
	flavor = daoyu_cheat
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		daoyu_primary_culture_count_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_country_has_primary_culture_more_than_one
		trigger = { var:daoyu_primary_culture_count > 1 scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { this = c:CHI } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#民族同化
		trigger = { var:daoyu_primary_culture_count = 1 scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { this = c:CHI } } }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_600 } } scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_variable = daoyu_all_owner_homeland } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#民族同化
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { this = c:CHI } }
		if = {
			limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_600 } }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { 
				set_variable = daoyu_all_owner_homeland
				if = { limit = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:manchu } remove_primary_culture = cu:manchu }
				if = { limit = { not = { country_has_primary_culture = cu:han } } add_primary_culture = cu:han }
				if = { limit = { exists = c:TIB c:TIB = { is_ai = yes } } annex = c:TIB }
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
	}
	after = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_300 }
				random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
				remove_global_variable = daoyu_300 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_500 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_500 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_600 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_600 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
}
#地区
daoyu.600 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = STATES
	flavor = daoyu_states_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = ai_goal_expand_resource_industries#扩大资源产业
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.610 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_goal_expand_agriculture#扩展农业
		trigger = { has_technology_researched = enclosure }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.615 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_goal_expand_factories#扩建工厂
		trigger = { has_technology_researched = enclosure }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.625 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_goal_expand_infrastructure#扩建基础设施
		trigger = { has_technology_researched = enclosure }
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.620 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_each_culture_of_state#地区民族
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.630 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporate_state#整合地区
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.640 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = STATE_TRAIT_STATE_MODIFIER#地区修正
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_migration#移民
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect#一键洗地
		if = {
			limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
			set_variable = daoyu_target_country
			set_global_variable = daoyu_600
			hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.590 popup = yes } }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = move_capital_lens_option#迁都
		set_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = move_market_capital_lens_option#迁移市场中心
		set_global_variable = daoyu_move_market
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = good_pollution_modifier#污染治理措施
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { state_region = { pollution_amount > 1 } } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { state_region = { pollution_amount > 1 } } state_region = { add_pollution = -100 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_radicals#激进主义者
		if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.604 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_solve_lag#低配置主机解决卡顿
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.690 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#地区
daoyu.601 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = STATES
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market }
					any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count > 1 }
				}
				desc = daoyu_error
			}
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } } desc = daoyu_error }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } desc = move_capital_lens_option }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } desc = move_market_capital_lens_option }
		}
	}
	flavor = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				trigger = {
					or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market }
					any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count > 1 }
				}
				desc = daoyu_multiple_target_state
			}
		}
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } } desc = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } desc = move_capital_lens_option } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } desc = move_market_capital_lens_option } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } desc = FROM } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } desc = daoyu_tst_1 } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } desc = TO } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } desc = daoyu_tst_2 } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } }
			random_scope_state = { limit = { is_capital = yes } save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_1 }
			random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#确认
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital_or_move_market
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital_or_move_market }
			daoyu_move_capital_or_move_market = yes
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital_or_move_market
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_market
		}
		trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes }
	}
}

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.631 popup = yes } }
	}

		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.630 popup = yes } }

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID#目标地区无效
		trigger = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.640 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporated_states#已整合地区
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state is_incorporated = no is_treaty_port = no } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state is_incorporated = no } set_state_type = incorporated }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_unincorporated_states#未整合地区
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state is_incorporated = yes } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state is_incorporated = yes } set_state_type = unincorporated }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
	}
	after = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
}

daoyu.650 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = STATE_TRAIT_STATE_MODIFIER
	flavor = daoyu_states_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { set_global_variable = daoyu_650 }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all_modifiers
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options }
			any_state = {
				or = {
					has_modifier = daoyu_state_negative_birth_rate_mult
					has_modifier = daoyu_state_positive_birth_rate_mult
					has_modifier = daoyu_growth_mortality
					has_modifier = daoyu_migration_pull
					has_modifier = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult
					has_modifier = daoyu_state_colony_growth
					has_modifier = daoyu_building_minimum_wage_mult
					has_modifier = daoyu_decree_road_maintenance
					has_modifier = daoyu_decree_promote_social_mobility
					has_modifier = daoyu_throughput_and_input_mult
					has_modifier = daoyu_decree_enlistment_efforts
				}
			}
		}
		daoyu_state_modifier_remove_modifier_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_state_negative_birth_rate_mult#负出生率
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_state_negative_birth_rate_mult

	}
	option = {

		set_global_variable = daoyu_growth_mortality

	}
	option = {
		name = modifier_building_minimum_wage_mult#最低工资
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_building_minimum_wage_mult
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_greener_grass_campaign#青草运动
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_migration_pull
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_promote_national_values#弘扬国家价值
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options } any_scope_state = { or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = modifier_state_colony_growth_creation_mult#殖民地增长产生
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options } any_scope_state = { any_neighbouring_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_adventitious_options#可多选的修正
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_promote_social_mobility#促进社会流动
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_decree_promote_social_mobility } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_decree_promote_social_mobility
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_road_maintenance#道路养护
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_decree_road_maintenance } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_decree_road_maintenance
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_throughput_and_input_mult#吞吐量
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_throughput_and_input_mult } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_throughput_and_input_mult
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_enlistment_efforts#征募努力
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_decree_enlistment_efforts } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_decree_enlistment_efforts
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#确认
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options
			or = {
				has_global_variable = daoyu_decree_promote_social_mobility
				has_global_variable = daoyu_decree_road_maintenance
				has_global_variable = daoyu_throughput_and_input_mult
				has_global_variable = daoyu_decree_enlistment_efforts
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options }
		daoyu_state_modifier_remove_global_variable_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options } }
		daoyu_state_modifier_remove_global_variable_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#地区修正
daoyu.655 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = STATE_TRAIT_STATE_MODIFIER
	flavor = daoyu_states_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = modifier_battle_combat_effectiveness_owned_province_mult#本国领土
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_state_modifier }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporated_state#已整合地区
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } }
			or = { any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = yes or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult } }
		}
		every_scope_state = { limit = { is_incorporated = yes } set_variable = daoyu_state_modifier }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID#目标地区无效
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } }
			or = {
				not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
				and = {
					has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult
					not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_daoyu_target_state#目标地区
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } }
			or = {
				and = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
				and = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult }
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult } }
			every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_state_modifier }
		}
		else = { every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } set_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	any_scope_state = { or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } }
	option = {
		name = 1x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "1" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 2x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "2" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 5x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "5" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 10x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "10" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 15x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "15" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 20x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "20" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 30x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "30" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 50x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "50" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 100x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "100" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		daoyu_state_modifier_remove_global_variable_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }

#移民
daoyu.660 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_migration
	flavor = daoyu_migration_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_state_1 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state not = { this = scope:daoyu_target_state_1 } } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_state_2 }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#移除目标国家
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID#目标国家无效
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 2 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID#目标地区无效
		trigger = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 2 } any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_cross_border_migration_target_state_not_valid#跨境移民(目标地区无效)
		trigger = { and = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_daoyu_target_state_1#失业
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { not = { this = scope:daoyu_target_state_1 } any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } add_pop_wealth = { wealth_distribution = { value = 5 } } move_pop = scope:daoyu_target_state_1 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_daoyu_target_country#失业人口送目标国家
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } any_scope_state = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } move_pop = scope:daoyu_target_country.capital } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_cross_border_migration#跨境移民
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.661 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_migration_from_A_to_B#
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 2 } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_1 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_from every_scope_culture = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_migration_from_B_to_A#
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 2 } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_from every_scope_culture = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_1 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.661 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_migration
	flavor = daoyu_migration_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_1 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_1 }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_2 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_2 }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_3 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_3 }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_4 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_4 }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_5 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_5 }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_6 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_6 }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_7 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_7 }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_8 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_8 }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_9 set_global_variable = daoyu_tst_9 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tst_1
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_1 }
		scope:daoyu_tst_1 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tst_2
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_2 }
		scope:daoyu_tst_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_state }

	option = {

	option = {
		name = ENCYCLOPEDIAGE_NEXT_PAGE
		trigger = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_661
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		set_global_variable = daoyu_660
	}
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_1 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_2 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_3
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_4 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_5 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_6

		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_660 }
			every_state = { remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_global_variable = daoyu_660 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes }
		}
		else = { every_state = { remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.662 popup = yes } }

	type = country_event

	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_migration
	flavor = daoyu_migration_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_state_1 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_state_2 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_migration_from_A_to_B#
		scope:daoyu_target_state_1 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_from every_scope_culture = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_migration_from_B_to_A#
		scope:daoyu_target_state_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_from every_scope_culture = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_1 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } remove_variable = daoyu_target_state }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.665 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_migration
	flavor = daoyu_migration_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_migration_from } save_scope_as = daoyu_migration_from }
		random_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to } save_scope_as = daoyu_migration_go_to }
		scope:daoyu_migration_from = { daoyu_migration_potential_target_effect = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_unemployed#失业
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { not = { this = scope:daoyu_target_state_1 } any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } }
		scope:daoyu_migration_from = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } add_pop_wealth = { wealth_distribution = { value = 5 } } move_pop = scope:daoyu_migration_go_to } }
		if = { limit = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } } set_global_variable = daoyu_662 }
		else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_660 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_1
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_1 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_1 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_2
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_2 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_3
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_3 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_3 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_4
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_4 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_4 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_5
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_5 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_5 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_6
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_6 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_6 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_7
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_7 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_7 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_8
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_8 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_8 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tcu_9
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_9 }
		scope:daoyu_tcu_9 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_culture } set_global_variable = daoyu_666
	}
	option = {
		name = ENCYCLOPEDIAGE_NEXT_PAGE
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_migration_from = { any_scope_culture = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_665
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		if = { limit = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } } set_global_variable = daoyu_662 }
		else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_660 }
	}
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_1 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_2 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_3
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_4 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_5 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_6
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_7 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_8 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_9
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_665 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_665 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
		else = {
			scope:daoyu_migration_from = { every_scope_culture = { remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
			scope:daoyu_migration_go_to = { every_scope_culture = { remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_666 }
				remove_global_variable = daoyu_666
				if = {
					limit = {
						scope:daoyu_migration_from = {
							any_scope_pop = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } save_temporary_scope_as = daoyu_any_pop }
							any_scope_pop = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } not = { religion = scope:daoyu_any_pop.religion } }
						}
					}
					trigger_event = { id = daoyu.666 popup = yes }
				}
				else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_from_665 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.667 popup = yes } }
			}
			else = {
				scope:daoyu_migration_from = { remove_variable = daoyu_migration_from } scope:daoyu_migration_go_to = { remove_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to }
				if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_660 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_660 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
				else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_662 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_662 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.662 popup = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
}

		daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = { TYPE = engineers }
		daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = { TYPE = capitalists }
		daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = { TYPE = bureaucrats }
		daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = { TYPE = aristocrats }
		daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = { TYPE = peasants }
		if = {
			limit = { scope:daoyu_migration_go_to = { owner = { has_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned } } }
			scope:daoyu_migration_from = { random_scope_pop = { daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = yes } }
		}
		else = { daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = { TYPE = slaves } }

		trigger = { daoyu_move_pop_religion_trigger = { TYPE = peasants } }
		daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = { TYPE = peasants }
	}
	option = {
		name = slaves_no_icon#奴隶
		trigger = { daoyu_move_pop_religion_trigger = { TYPE = slaves } }
		if = {
			limit = { scope:daoyu_migration_go_to = { owner = { has_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned } } }
			scope:daoyu_migration_from = {
				random_scope_pop = {
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = catholic }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = protestant }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = orthodox }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = oriental_orthodox }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = sunni }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = shiite }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = jewish }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = mahayana }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = gelugpa }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = theravada }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = confucian }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = hindu }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = shinto }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = sikh }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = animist }
					daoyu_move_pop_religion_slaves_effect = { RELIGION = atheist }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { daoyu_move_pop_religion_effect = { TYPE = slaves } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		scope:daoyu_migration_from = { every_scope_culture = { remove_variable = daoyu_target_pop } }
		scope:daoyu_migration_go_to = { every_scope_culture = { remove_variable = daoyu_target_pop } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_665 }
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_from_665 set_global_variable = daoyu_665
			scope:daoyu_migration_from = { every_scope_culture = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target remove_variable = daoyu_target_culture } }
			scope:daoyu_migration_go_to = { every_scope_culture = { remove_variable = daoyu_target_culture } }
		}
		else = {
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_catholic
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_protestant
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_orthodox
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_oriental_orthodox
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_sunni
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_shiite
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_jewish
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_mahayana
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_gelugpa
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_theravada
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_confucian
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_hindu
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_shinto
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_sikh
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_animist
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_pop_atheist
			set_global_variable = daoyu_666
		}
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_665 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_665 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_666 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_666 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.666 popup = yes } }
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.667 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.690 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_solve_lag
	flavor = daoyu_one_building_one_region_flavor
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } } desc = daoyu_one_building_one_region_flavor } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } desc = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all#移除全部
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait
			or = {
				daoyu_resources_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
				daoyu_agriculture_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
				daoyu_industry_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		daoyu_remove_all_building_state_trait = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.690 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = resources_lens_tab#资源
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait daoyu_resources_building_state_trait_trigger = yes }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } } set_global_variable = daoyu_add_building_state_trait }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.691 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = agriculture_lens_tab#农业
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait daoyu_agriculture_building_state_trait_trigger = yes }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } } set_global_variable = daoyu_add_building_state_trait }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.692 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = industry_lens_tab#工业
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait daoyu_industry_building_state_trait_trigger = yes }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } } set_global_variable = daoyu_add_building_state_trait }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.693 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = resources_lens_tab#资源
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_add_building_state_trait
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.691 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = agriculture_lens_tab#农业
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_add_building_state_trait
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.692 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = industry_lens_tab#工业
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_add_building_state_trait
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.693 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait#删除地区特质
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait }
			or = {
				daoyu_resources_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
				daoyu_agriculture_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
				daoyu_industry_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.690 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on
		trigger = {
			nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait has_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on }
			or = {
				daoyu_resources_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
				daoyu_agriculture_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
				daoyu_industry_building_state_trait_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.690 popup = yes } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.699 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_one_building_one_region_off
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.690 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}

			else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_693 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_693 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.693 popup = yes } }
		}

			remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_1 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_2 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_3

			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_2 } scope:daoyu_tst_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }

			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_4 } scope:daoyu_tst_4 = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }

			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_7 } scope:daoyu_tst_7 = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }

			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_9 } scope:daoyu_tst_9 = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_695 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.695 popup = yes }
		}

daoyu.699 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	hidden = yes
	trigger = { is_ai = no }
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_building_one_region_on }
			daoyu_one_building_one_region_effect = yes
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.699 days = 30 }
		}
	}
}

			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_country_add_radicals }

			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes or = { any_scope_state = { count > 4 } country_rank >= rank_value:minor_power } }
				add_treasury = -1000000
				every_scope_state = { daoyu_add_radicals_in_state_effect = yes }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes country_rank = rank_value:great_power }
				trigger_event = { id = daoyu.951 }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { owner = { or = { is_ai = no not = { country_rank = rank_value:great_power } } } has_variable = daoyu_deactivate_barracks }
				remove_variable = daoyu_deactivate_barracks activate_building = { building = building_barracks }
			}

		else = {
			every_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_deactivate_barracks } remove_variable = daoyu_deactivate_barracks activate_building = { building = building_barracks } }

			}

		}
	}

				if = {

		else_if = {

			daoyu_modifier_remove_modifier_effect = yes
			daoyu_state_modifier_remove_modifier_effect = yes
			every_country = { every_interest_group = { daoyu_remove_interest_group_approval_effcet = yes daoyu_remove_interest_group_pol_str_effcet = yes } }
		}
	}
